function change_target_specie(){
	var group=$("#pair_group option:selected").text();
if(group=="BOP clade"){$("#pair_specie1").html("<option value='Bdi'>Brachypodium distachyon</option><option value='Bsa'>Brachypodium stacei</option><option value='Hvu'>Hordeum vulgare</option><option arabicum</option><option value='Aha'>Arabidopsis halleri</option><option value='Aly'>Arabidopsis lyrata</option><option value='Ath'>Arabidopsis thaliana</option><option value='Aal'>Arabis alpina</option><option value='Bst'>Boechera stricta</option><option value='Bna'>Brassica napus</option><option value='Bol'>Brassica oleracea</option><option value='Bra'>Brassica rapa</option><option value='Cas'>Camelina sativa</option><option value='Cgr'>Capsella grandiflora</option><option value='Cru'>Capsella rubella</option><option value='Cpa'>Carica papaya</option><option value='Esa'>Eutrema salsugineum</option><option value='Rsa'>Raphanus sativus</option><option value='Sir'>Sisymbrium irio</option><option value='Tha'>Tarenaya hassleriana</option><option value='Tpa'>Thellungiella parvula</option>");}if(group=="Fabales"){$("#pair_specie1").html("<option value='Adu'>Arachis duranensis</option><option value='Aip'>Arachis ipaensis</option><option value='Cca'>Cajanus cajan</option><option value='Car'>Cicer arietinum</option><option value='Gma'>Glycine max</option><option value='Gso'>Glycine soja</option><option value='Lja'>Lotus japonicus</option><option value='Mtr'>Medicago truncatula</option><option value='Pvu'>Phaseolus vulgaris</option><option value='Tpr'>Trifolium pratense</option><option value='Van'>Vigna angularis</option><option value='Vra'>Vigna radiata</option>");}if(group=="Lamiales"){$("#pair_specie1").html("<option value='Dhy'>Dorcoceras hygrometricum</option><option value='Mgu'>Mimulus guttatus</option><option value='Sin'>Sesamum indicum</option><option value='Ugi'>Utricularia gibba</option>");}if(group=="Malpighiales"){$("#pair_specie1").html("<option value='Lus'>Linum usitatissimum</option><option value='Mes'>Manihot esculenta</option><option value='Ptr'>Populus trichocarpa</option><option value='Rco'>Ricinus communis</option><option value='Spu'>Salix purpurea</option>");}if(group=="PACMAD mays</option><option value='Zpa'>Zoysia pacifica</option>");}if(group=="Rosales"){$("#pair_specie1").html("<option value='Fve'>Fragaria vesca</option><option value='Mno'>Morus notabilis</option><option value='Pmu'>Prunus mume</option><option value='Ppe'>Prunus persica</option><option value='Pbr'>Pyrus bretschneideri</option><option value='Zju'>Ziziphus jujuba</option>");}if(group=="Solanales"){$("#pair_specie1").html("<option value='Sly'>Solanum lycopersicum</option><option value='Stu'>Solanum tuberosum</option>");}change_query_specie();
}

function change_query_specie(){

function download_pair(){
	var value1=$("#pair_specie1").val();
	var value2=$("#pair_specie2").val();
	var type=$("#pair_type").val();
	window.location.href="/download_ftp.php?filepath=08-download/FTP/pairwise_alignments/"+value1+"/"+value1+"_"+value2+"."+type+".gz";
}
function download_mult(){
	var value1=$("#mult_specie option:selected").text();
	var value2=$("#mult_specie").val();
	if (value2=="Osj"){
		value1="Oryza_sativa_Japonica_Group";
	}
	window.location.href="/download_ftp.php?filepath=08-download/"+value1.replace(" ","_")+"/multiple_alignments/"+value2+".maf.gz";
}
function download_cons(){
	var value1=$("#cons_specie option:selected").text();
	var value2=$("#cons_specie").val();
	if (value2=="Osj"){
		value1="Oryza_sativa_Japonica_Group";
	}
	var type=$("#cons_type").val();
	window.location.href="/download_ftp.php?filepath=08-download/"+value1.replace(" ","_")+"/sequence_conservation/"+value2+"_"+type+".bedGraph.gz";
}


function download_rbh(){
	var value1=$("#specie1").val();
	var value2=$("#specie2").val();
	window.location.href="ftp://ftp.cbi.pku.edu.cn/pub/database/PlantRegMap/RBH/"+value1+"/"+value1+"_"+value2+"_RBH.list.gz";
}
function change_specie2(){
	$("#specie2").children("option").each(function(){
		$(this).show();
	});
	var value1=$("#specie1").val();
	$("#specie2 option[value='"+value1+"']").hide();
	if(value1=="Ath"){
		$('#specie2 option:eq(0)').prop('selected',false);
		$('#specie2 option:eq(1)').prop('selected',true);
	}
	else{
		$('#specie2 option:eq(1)').prop('selected',false);
		$('#specie2 option:eq(0)').prop('selected',true);
	}
}


// written by yangdc at 2016.9.14 it's useful but too lazy to handle the exception...
// usagemc(tableId, startRow, endRow, startCol,endCol);the first para is the id of your table and  the other four paras control the scope
function mc(tableId, startRow, endRow, startCol,endCol) { 
var tb = document.getElementById(tableId); 
if(startCol>tb.rows[0].cells.length-1){
	return;
}
if(startRow>tb.rows.length-1){
	return;
}
if (endCol == -1) { 
	endCol=tb.rows[0].cells.length-1;
} 
if (endRow == -1) {
	endRow = tb.rows.length-1; 
} 
var col=endCol;
var startrow=startRow;
for (var i = startRow; i < endRow; i++) { 
if (tb.rows[startRow].cells[col].innerHTML == tb.rows[i + 1].cells[col].innerHTML) { 
tb.rows[i + 1].removeChild(tb.rows[i + 1].cells[col]); 
tb.rows[startRow].cells[col].rowSpan = (tb.rows[startRow].cells[col].rowSpan | 0) + 1; 
 
}else { 
startRow = i + 1; 
mc(tableId, startRow, endRow , col , col); 
break;
}
}

if(startCol < col){
	col=col-1;
mc(tableId, startrow, endRow , startCol , col); 	
}

} 
$(function(){
mc('Cis-elements-dhs-table',0,-1,0,1); 
mc('Cis-elements-dgf-table',0,-1,0,1); 
mc('Cis-elements-hm-table',0,-1,0,1); 
mc('Cis-elements-np-table',0,-1,0,1);
mc('Cis-elements-tfbs-table',0,-1,5,5); 
mc('Cis-elements-tfbs-table',0,-1,0,1); 
mc('Cis-elements-ce-table',0,-1,0,1);

change_specie2(); 

$("#pair_specie1").val("Ath");
change_query_specie();

});
</script>
